## Installation & Usage
### pip install

If the python package is hosted on a repository, you can install directly using:

```sh
pip install git+https://github.com/kubernetes-client/python.git
```
(you may need to run `pip` with root permission: `sudo pip install git+https://github.com/kubernetes-client/python.git`)

Then import the package:
```python
import kubernetes.client
```

### Setuptools

Install via [Setuptools](http://pypi.python.org/pypi/setuptools).

```sh
python setup.py install --user
```
(or `sudo python setup.py install` to install the package for all users)

Then import the package:
```python
import kubernetes.client
```

Valid values are: - Ignore: This will ignore any unknown fields that are silently dropped from the object, and will ignore all but the last duplicate field that the decoder encounters. ## Documentation For Authorization


## BearerToken

- **Type**: API key
- **API key parameter name**: authorization
- **Location**: HTTP header
